=========================================================================\n * File:    include/eduledger/events.h\n * Purpose: Canonical event definitions for Payment-Saga bounded context\n * Author:  EduPay Ledger Academy \u2013 Lesson 06\n * ========================================================================= */\n#ifndef EDU_LEDGER_EVENTS_H\n#define EDU_LEDGER_EVENTS_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef enum {\n    EVT_NONE = 0,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_INITIATED,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_AUTHORIZED,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_CAPTURED,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_SETTLED,\n    EVT_PAYMENT_FAILED,\n} evt_type_t;\n\n/* Every event carries a header for routing & traceability */\ntypedef struct {\n    uint64_t    sequence;   /* monotonic sequence number from Event Store */\n    evt_type_t  type;       /* domain event discriminator                */\n    time_t      ts_utc;     /* server-side timestamp, seconds since EPOCH*/\n    char        saga_id[40];/* distributed-tx correlation id (UUID-v4)   */\n} evt_header_t;\n\n/* Event payloads --------------------------------------------------------- */\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         payment_id[32];\n    char         student_id[32];\n    char         currency[4]; /* ISO-4217 */\n    uint64_t     amount_minor;/* minor units e.g. cents */\n} evt_payment_initiated_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         payment_id[32];\n    char         authorization_code[16];\n} evt_payment_authorized_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         payment_id[32];\n    uint64_t     fee_minor;\n} evt_payment_captured_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         payment_id[32];\n    char         settlement_batch_id[32];\n} evt_payment_settled_t;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         payment_id[32];\n    char         reason[128];\n} evt_payment_failed_t;\n\n/* A convenience union for generic handlers */\ntypedef union {\n    evt_header_t               any;\n    evt_payment_initiated_t    initiated;\n    evt_payment_authorized_t   authorized;\n    evt_payment_captured_t     captured;\n    evt_payment_settled_t      settled;\n    evt_payment_failed_t       failed;\n} ledger_event_t;\n\n#endif /* EDU_LEDGER_EVENTS_H */\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4  Projection Port (Header Only)\n\nDefine a **Clean-Architecture port** so that multiple storage\u2010specific adapters can plug in.\n\n```c\n/* =========================================================================\n * File:    include/eduledger/projection.h\n * Purpose: Projection interface for CQRS read models\n * ========================================================================= */\n#ifndef EDU_LEDGER_PROJECTION_H\n#define EDU_LEDGER_PROJECTION_H\n\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n#include \"eduledger/events.h\"\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\nextern \"C\" {\n#endif\n\ntypedef struct ledger_projection ledger_projection_t;\n\n/* Factory function pointer table */\ntypedef struct {\n    ledger_projection_t* (*open)(const char* dsn, char* errbuf, size_t errlen);\n    void                 (*close)(ledger_projection_t*);\n    bool                 (*handle_event)(ledger_projection_t*, const ledger_event_t*, char* errbuf, size_t errlen);\n    uint64_t             (*last_sequence)(ledger_projection_t*);\n} ledger_projection_vtable_t;\n\n/* Adapter registration (one per .so or static obj) */\nbool register_ledger_projection(const ledger_projection_vtable_t* vtable);\n\n/* Global factory helpers ------------------------------------------------- */\nledger_projection_t* projection_open(const char* dsn, char* errbuf, size_t errlen);\nvoid                 projection_close(ledger_projection_t* proj);\nbool                 projection_handle_event(ledger_projection_t* proj, const ledger_event_t* evt, char* errbuf, size_t errlen);\nuint64_t             projection_last_sequence(ledger_projection_t* proj);\n\n#ifdef __cplusplus\n}\n#endif\n#endif /* EDU_LEDGER_PROJECTION_H */\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5  In-Memory Stub (Unit-Test Harness)\n\nQuickly confirm our port by building an **In-Memory projection** before adding SQLite.\n\n```c\n/* =========================================================================\n * File:    src/eduledger/projection_mem.c\n * Purpose: In-Memory projection for fast CI pipelines\n * ========================================================================= */\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"eduledger/projection.h\"\n\ntypedef struct {\n    ledger_projection_t base;\n    uint64_t            cursor;\n    size_t              payments_total;\n} mem_proj_t;\n\n/* --- Interface implementations ----------------------------------------- */\nstatic ledger_projection_t* mem_open(const char* dsn, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    (void)dsn; /* not used */\n    mem_proj_t* p = calloc(1, sizeof *p);\n    if (!p) {\n        strncpy(err, \"OOM opening mem projection\", len);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n    return (ledger_projection_t*)p;\n}\n\nstatic void mem_close(ledger_projection_t* obj)\n{\n    free(obj);\n}\n\nstatic bool mem_handle(ledger_projection_t* obj, const ledger_event_t* evt, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    (void)err; (void)len;\n    mem_proj_t* p = (mem_proj_t*)obj;\n    /* idempotency: ignore older sequences */\n    if (evt->any.hdr.sequence <= p->cursor) return true;\n\n    switch (evt->any.hdr.type) {\n        case EVT_PAYMENT_INITIATED:\n            p->payments_total++;\n            break;\n        default:\n            /* other events ignored for demo */\n            break;\n    }\n    p->cursor = evt->any.hdr.sequence;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic uint64_t mem_last(ledger_projection_t* obj)\n{\n    mem_proj_t* p = (mem_proj_t*)obj;\n    return p->cursor;\n}\n\n/* --- VTable registration ----------------------------------------------- */\nstatic const ledger_projection_vtable_t VTABLE = {\n    .open          = mem_open,\n    .close         = mem_close,\n    .handle_event  = mem_handle,\n    .last_sequence = mem_last,\n};\n\n/* Register at load time (constructor attr works on gcc/clang) */\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void register_mem_projection(void)\n{\n    register_ledger_projection(&VTABLE);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6  SQLite3 Production Adapter\n\nThe in-memory version is fine for CI but prod needs durability.   \nBelow is a fully functional **SQLite3 projection** with _idempotent upserts_ and **optimistic concurrency**.\n\n```c\n/* =========================================================================\n * File:    src/eduledger/projection_sqlite.c\n * Purpose: Durable CQRS read model stored in SQLite\n * ========================================================================= */\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include <sqlite3.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"eduledger/projection.h\"\n\n#ifndef EDU_SQL_SCHEMA\n#define EDU_SQL_SCHEMA                                                     \\\n    \"PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL;\"                                             \\\n    \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projection_cursor(\"                        \\\n    \"   id       INTEGER PRIMARY KEY CHECK (id = 0),\"                      \\\n    \"   seq      INTEGER NOT NULL\"                                         \\\n    \");\"                                                                   \\\n    \"INSERT OR IGNORE INTO projection_cursor(id, seq) VALUES(0, 0);\"       \\\n    \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS vw_payments(\"                              \\\n    \"   payment_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\"                                      \\\n    \"   student_id TEXT NOT NULL,\"                                         \\\n    \"   currency   TEXT NOT NULL,\"                                         \\\n    \"   amount_minor INTEGER NOT NULL,\"                                    \\\n    \"   status     TEXT NOT NULL,\"                                         \\\n    \"   last_event_seq INTEGER NOT NULL\"                                   \\\n    \");\"\n#endif /* EDU_SQL_SCHEMA */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    ledger_projection_t base;\n    sqlite3*            db;\n} sqlite_proj_t;\n\n/* Error helper ----------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic bool sqlite_check(int rc, sqlite3* db, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    if (rc == SQLITE_OK || rc == SQLITE_DONE || rc == SQLITE_ROW) return true;\n    snprintf(err, len, \"SQLite error %d: %s\", rc, sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n    return false;\n}\n\n/* --- Interface implementations ----------------------------------------- */\nstatic ledger_projection_t* s_open(const char* dsn, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    sqlite3* db = NULL;\n    int rc = sqlite3_open_v2(dsn ? dsn : \":memory:\",\n                             &db,\n                             SQLITE_OPEN_READWRITE | SQLITE_OPEN_CREATE | SQLITE_OPEN_FULLMUTEX,\n                             NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, db, err, len)) return NULL;\n\n    rc = sqlite3_exec(db, EDU_SQL_SCHEMA, NULL, NULL, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, db, err, len)) { sqlite3_close(db); return NULL; }\n\n    sqlite_proj_t* p = calloc(1, sizeof *p);\n    if (!p) { strncpy(err, \"OOM\", len); sqlite3_close(db); return NULL; }\n    p->db = db;\n    return (ledger_projection_t*)p;\n}\n\nstatic void s_close(ledger_projection_t* obj)\n{\n    sqlite_proj_t* p = (sqlite_proj_t*)obj;\n    if (!p) return;\n    sqlite3_close(p->db);\n    free(p);\n}\n\nstatic uint64_t s_last(ledger_projection_t* obj)\n{\n    sqlite_proj_t* p = (sqlite_proj_t*)obj;\n    uint64_t seq = 0;\n    sqlite3_stmt* stmt = NULL;\n    const char* sql = \"SELECT seq FROM projection_cursor WHERE id = 0;\";\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(p->db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) == SQLITE_OK &&\n        sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW)\n    {\n        seq = (uint64_t)sqlite3_column_int64(stmt, 0);\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return seq;\n}\n\nstatic bool s_update_cursor(sqlite_proj_t* p, uint64_t seq, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    sqlite3_stmt* stmt = NULL;\n    const char* sql = \"UPDATE projection_cursor SET seq = ? WHERE id = 0;\";\n    int rc = sqlite3_prepare_v2(p->db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len)) return false;\n\n    sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 1, (sqlite3_int64)seq);\n    rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len);\n}\n\nstatic bool handle_payment_initiated(sqlite_proj_t* p,\n                                     const evt_payment_initiated_t* e,\n                                     char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    const char* sql =\n        \"INSERT INTO vw_payments(payment_id, student_id, currency, amount_minor, status, last_event_seq) \"\n        \"VALUES(?, ?, ?, ?, 'INITIATED', ?)\"\n        \"ON CONFLICT(payment_id) DO UPDATE SET \"\n        \"  student_id=excluded.student_id,\"\n        \"  currency=excluded.currency,\"\n        \"  amount_minor=excluded.amount_minor,\"\n        \"  status='INITIATED',\"\n        \"  last_event_seq=excluded.last_event_seq \"\n        \"WHERE excluded.last_event_seq > vw_payments.last_event_seq;\";\n\n    sqlite3_stmt* stmt = NULL;\n    int rc = sqlite3_prepare_v2(p->db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len)) return false;\n\n    sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, 1, e->payment_id, -1, SQLITE_STATIC);\n    sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, 2, e->student_id, -1, SQLITE_STATIC);\n    sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, 3, e->currency, -1, SQLITE_STATIC);\n    sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 4, (sqlite3_int64)e->amount_minor);\n    sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 5, (sqlite3_int64)e->hdr.sequence);\n\n    rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len);\n}\n\nstatic bool handle_payment_settled(sqlite_proj_t* p,\n                                   const evt_payment_settled_t* e,\n                                   char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    const char* sql =\n        \"UPDATE vw_payments SET status='SETTLED', last_event_seq=? \"\n        \"WHERE payment_id=? AND ? > last_event_seq;\";\n\n    sqlite3_stmt* stmt = NULL;\n    int rc = sqlite3_prepare_v2(p->db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len)) return false;\n\n    sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 1, (sqlite3_int64)e->hdr.sequence);\n    sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, 2, e->payment_id, -1, SQLITE_STATIC);\n    sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt, 3, (sqlite3_int64)e->hdr.sequence);\n\n    rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len);\n}\n\nstatic bool s_handle(ledger_projection_t* obj, const ledger_event_t* e, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    sqlite_proj_t* p = (sqlite_proj_t*)obj;\n\n    /* idempotency short-circuit */\n    if (e->any.hdr.sequence <= s_last(obj)) return true;\n\n    int rc = sqlite3_exec(p->db, \"BEGIN IMMEDIATE TRANSACTION;\", NULL, NULL, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len)) return false;\n\n    bool ok = true;\n    switch (e->any.hdr.type) {\n        case EVT_PAYMENT_INITIATED:\n            ok = handle_payment_initiated(p, &e->initiated, err, len);\n            break;\n        case EVT_PAYMENT_SETTLED:\n            ok = handle_payment_settled(p, &e->settled, err, len);\n            break;\n        default:\n            /* unsupported events are ignored for this projection */\n            break;\n    }\n\n    if (ok) ok = s_update_cursor(p, e->any.hdr.sequence, err, len);\n\n    rc = sqlite3_exec(p->db, ok ? \"COMMIT;\" : \"ROLLBACK;\", NULL, NULL, NULL);\n    if (!sqlite_check(rc, p->db, err, len)) ok = false;\n\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/* --- VTable registration ----------------------------------------------- */\nstatic const ledger_projection_vtable_t VTABLE = {\n    .open          = s_open,\n    .close         = s_close,\n    .handle_event  = s_handle,\n    .last_sequence = s_last,\n};\n\n__attribute__((constructor))\nstatic void register_sqlite_projection(void)\n{\n    register_ledger_projection(&VTABLE);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7  Projection Registry (Shared)\n\nAll adapters share a **singleton registry** so the application can load whichever is linked first.\n\n```c\n/* =========================================================================\n * File:    src/eduledger/projection_registry.c\n * Purpose: Adapter registry \u2013 decouples caller from implementation\n * ========================================================================= */\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"eduledger/projection.h\"\n\nstatic pthread_mutex_t                lock = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;\nstatic const ledger_projection_vtable_t* active = NULL;\n\nbool register_ledger_projection(const ledger_projection_vtable_t* vtable)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&lock);\n    if (!active) active = vtable; /* first wins */\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&lock);\n    return true;\n}\n\nledger_projection_t* projection_open(const char* dsn, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    if (!active) { strncpy(err, \"No projection adapter registered\", len); return NULL; }\n    return active->open(dsn, err, len);\n}\n\nvoid projection_close(ledger_projection_t* p)\n{\n    if (p && active) active->close(p);\n}\n\nbool projection_handle_event(ledger_projection_t* p, const ledger_event_t* e, char* err, size_t len)\n{\n    return p && active && active->handle_event(p, e, err, len);\n}\n\nuint64_t projection_last_sequence(ledger_projection_t* p)\n{\n    return (p && active) ? active->last_sequence(p) : 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8  Driver Loop Example\n\nThe event store will invoke `projection_handle_event()` for each new commit.  \nFor local testing we bundle a minimal CLI.\n\n```c\n/* =========================================================================\n * File:    apps/projection_cli.c\n * Purpose: Stand-alone tool to hydrate a projection DB from an event log\n * ========================================================================= */\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include \"eduledger/projection.h\"\n\nstatic void die(const char* msg)\n{\n    fprintf(stderr, \"fatal: %s\\n\", msg);\n    exit(EXIT_FAILURE);\n}\n\n/* Simulate reading newline-delimited events from stdin */\nstatic ledger_event_t parse_event(const char* line)\n{\n    ledger_event_t e = {0};\n    /* CSV: seq,type,payment,student,amount */\n    sscanf(line, \"%lu,%d,%31[^,],%31[^,],%lu\",\n           &e.any.hdr.sequence,\n           (int*)&e.any.hdr.type,\n           e.initiated.payment_id,\n           e.initiated.student_id,\n           &e.initiated.amount_minor);\n    e.any.hdr.ts_utc = time(NULL);\n    strcpy(e.initiated.currency, \"USD\");\n    return e;\n}\n\nint main(int argc, char* argv[])\n{\n    char err[256] = {0};\n    const char* dsn = argc > 1 ? argv[1] : \"file:projection.db?cache=shared\";\n\n    ledger_projection_t* p = projection_open(dsn, err, sizeof err);\n    if (!p) die(err);\n\n    char*  line = NULL;\n    size_t n    = 0;\n    while (getline(&line, &n, stdin) != -1) {\n        ledger_event_t evt = parse_event(line);\n        if (!projection_handle_event(p, &evt, err, sizeof err))\n            die(err);\n    }\n    free(line);\n\n    printf(\"Projection at sequence %lu\\n\", projection_last_sequence(p));\n    projection_close(p);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9  Compilation (GNU Make)\n\n```make\nCC      ?= gcc\nCFLAGS  := -std=c17 -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -O2 -fPIC\nLDFLAGS := -lsqlite3 -lpthread\n\nSRC := $(shell find src -name '*.c')\nOBJ := $(SRC:.c=.o)\n\nall: projection_cli\n\nprojection_cli: $(OBJ) apps/projection_cli.o\n\t$(CC) $^ $(LDFLAGS) -o $@\n\n%.o: %.c\n\t$(CC) $(CFLAGS) -Iinclude -c $< -o $@\n\nclean:\n\trm -f $(OBJ) apps/*.o projection_cli projection.db\n```\n\n---\n\n## 10  Exercises\n\n1. Implement support for `EVT_PAYMENT_FAILED` and update the dashboard schema accordingly.  \n2. Add a **Prometheus** exporter that reports `projection_lag_seconds = now() \u2013 last_event.ts_utc`.  \n3. Swap SQLite for **PostgreSQL** by writing a new adapter conforming to `ledger_projection_vtable_t`.\n\nHappy projecting! \ud83d\ude80\n```",

The saga coordinates the following participating services:\n *\n *          1. Compliance/KYC          \u2013 FERPA-aware identity & sanction checks\n *          2. Payment Gateway         \u2013 Reserve + capture funds\n *          3. Ledger Repository       \u2013 Immutable, event-sourced ledger entry\n *          4. Stipend Repository      \u2013 Aggregate root for stipend domain\n *          5. Event Bus               \u2013 Publishes domain & integration events\n *          6. Audit Logger            \u2013 Immutable audit trail\n *\n *      Compensating transactions are issued on failure so that the system\n *      remains eventually consistent across micro-services.\n *\n *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n */\n\n#include <errno.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\n#include \"domain/models/stipend_request.h\"\n#include \"domain/events/stipend_events.h\"\n\n#include \"application/ports/repositories/ledger_repository.h\"\n#include \"application/ports/repositories/stipend_repository.h\"\n\n#include \"application/ports/services/compliance_service.h\"\n#include \"application/ports/services/payment_gateway.h\"\n\n#include \"application/ports/messaging/event_bus.h\"\n#include \"application/ports/audit/audit_logger.h\"\n\n#include \"utils/retry_policy.h\"\n#include \"utils/uuid.h\"\n#include \"utils/timestamp.h\"\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Constants & Macros                                                        */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n#define SAGA_TAG             \"DISBURSE_STIPEND_SAGA\"\n#define SAGA_VERSION         \"v1.0.0\"\n#define SAGA_MAX_STEP_NAME   48\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Enumerations                                                              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntypedef enum\n{\n    SAGA_STATE_NOT_STARTED = 0,\n    SAGA_STATE_COMPLIANCE_PASSED,\n    SAGA_STATE_FUNDS_RESERVED,\n    SAGA_STATE_LEDGER_POSTED,\n    SAGA_STATE_DISBURSED,\n    SAGA_STATE_ROLLING_BACK,\n    SAGA_STATE_FAILED,\n    SAGA_STATE_COMPLETED\n} saga_state_e;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Data Structures                                                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Forward declaration of self for step function pointer typedef */\nstruct disburse_stipend_saga_s;\n\n/* Step/compensation function pointer */\ntypedef bool (*saga_step_fn)(struct disburse_stipend_saga_s *saga);\n\n/* Step registration */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    char         name[SAGA_MAX_STEP_NAME];\n    saga_step_fn forward;\n    saga_step_fn compensate;\n} saga_step_t;\n\n/* Disburse Stipend Saga aggregate */\ntypedef struct disburse_stipend_saga_s\n{\n    /* Ports (dependency inversion) */\n    compliance_service_t  *compliance;\n    payment_gateway_t     *gateway;\n    ledger_repository_t   *ledger_repo;\n    stipend_repository_t  *stipend_repo;\n    event_bus_t           *event_bus;\n    audit_logger_t        *audit;\n\n    /* Saga metadata */\n    char           saga_id[UUID_STR_LEN];\n    saga_state_e   state;\n    retry_policy_t retry_policy;\n    timestamp_t    started_at;\n\n    /* Domain input */\n    const stipend_request_t *request;\n\n    /* Internal workflow */\n    size_t        step_count;\n    saga_step_t  *steps;\n} disburse_stipend_saga_t;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Utility \u2013 Error & Audit Helpers                                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic void\nsaga_log_audit(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga,\n               audit_severity_e         severity,\n               const char              *fmt,\n               ...)\n{\n    if (!saga || !saga->audit) { return; }\n\n    va_list args;\n    va_start(args, fmt);\n    audit_logger_vlog(saga->audit, severity, SAGA_TAG, saga->saga_id, fmt, args);\n    va_end(args);\n}\n\nstatic void\nsaga_publish_event(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga,\n                   const stipend_event_t   *event)\n{\n    if (!saga || !saga->event_bus || !event) { return; }\n\n    event_bus_publish(saga->event_bus, (const event_base_t *)event);\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Forward Step Implementations                                              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* ---- Step 1: Compliance Check ------------------------------------------- */\nstatic bool\nstep_compliance_check(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    stipend_event_t ev = {0};\n\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Running compliance checks\u2026\");\n\n    compliance_result_t res = compliance_service_check(\n        saga->compliance,\n        &saga->request->student,\n        &saga->request->payout_details);\n\n    if (res.status != COMPLIANCE_STATUS_OK)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_WARN,\n                       \"Compliance check failed \u2014 reason: %s\",\n                       res.reason);\n\n        ev.type              = STIPEND_EVENT_COMPLIANCE_FAILED;\n        ev.stipend_request   = *saga->request;\n        strncpy(ev.reason, res.reason, sizeof(ev.reason) - 1);\n        saga_publish_event(saga, &ev);\n\n        errno = EACCES; /* Permission denied / non-compliant */\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Compliance passed.\");\n    ev.type            = STIPEND_EVENT_COMPLIANCE_PASSED;\n    ev.stipend_request = *saga->request;\n    saga_publish_event(saga, &ev);\n\n    saga->state = SAGA_STATE_COMPLIANCE_PASSED;\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* Compensation: no action needed for compliance                            */\nstatic bool\ncompensate_compliance(__attribute__((unused)) disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    return true; /* Idempotent \u2013 nothing to undo */\n}\n\n/* ---- Step 2: Reserve Funds ---------------------------------------------- */\nstatic bool\nstep_reserve_funds(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Reserving funds\u2026\");\n\n    payment_reservation_t reservation = {0};\n    int rc = payment_gateway_reserve(\n        saga->gateway,\n        &saga->request->payout_details,\n        &reservation);\n\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Fund reservation failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        errno = rc;\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Persist reservation token on stipend aggregate for later capture */\n    stipend_repository_attach_reservation(\n        saga->stipend_repo,\n        saga->request->stipend_id,\n        &reservation);\n\n    saga->state = SAGA_STATE_FUNDS_RESERVED;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic bool\ncompensate_reserve_funds(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    /* Release reservation only if it exists */\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Releasing reserved funds (rollback)\u2026\");\n\n    /* Retrieve token back from stipend aggregate */\n    payment_reservation_t token = {0};\n    int rc = stipend_repository_get_reservation(\n        saga->stipend_repo,\n        saga->request->stipend_id,\n        &token);\n\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Failed to fetch reservation token (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    rc = payment_gateway_release(saga->gateway, &token);\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Fund release failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* ---- Step 3: Ledger Posting --------------------------------------------- */\nstatic bool\nstep_ledger_post(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Posting ledger entry\u2026\");\n\n    ledger_entry_t entry = {\n        .entry_id       = \"\",\n        .timestamp      = timestamp_now(),\n        .type           = LEDGER_ENTRY_STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT,\n        .amount         = saga->request->payout_details.amount,\n        .currency       = saga->request->payout_details.currency,\n        .student_id     = saga->request->student.student_id,\n        .correlation_id = saga->saga_id\n    };\n\n    uuid_generate(entry.entry_id, sizeof(entry.entry_id));\n\n    int rc = ledger_repository_append(saga->ledger_repo, &entry);\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Ledger append failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        errno = rc;\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    saga->state = SAGA_STATE_LEDGER_POSTED;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic bool\ncompensate_ledger_post(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Reversing ledger entry (rollback)\u2026\");\n\n    int rc = ledger_repository_reversal(\n        saga->ledger_repo,\n        saga->request->student.student_id,\n        saga->saga_id); /* correlation_id */\n\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Ledger reversal failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* ---- Step 4: Capture / Disburse Funds ------------------------------------ */\nstatic bool\nstep_capture_funds(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Capturing reserved funds to student account\u2026\");\n\n    payment_reservation_t token = {0};\n    int rc = stipend_repository_get_reservation(\n        saga->stipend_repo,\n        saga->request->stipend_id,\n        &token);\n\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Reservation token missing (err=%d)\", rc);\n        errno = rc;\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    rc = payment_gateway_capture(saga->gateway, &token);\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Fund capture failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        errno = rc;\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    saga->state = SAGA_STATE_DISBURSED;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic bool\ncompensate_capture_funds(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    /* Attempt refund only if capture was successful */\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Refunding captured funds (rollback)\u2026\");\n\n    payment_reservation_t token = {0};\n    int rc = stipend_repository_get_reservation(\n        saga->stipend_repo,\n        saga->request->stipend_id,\n        &token);\n\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Reservation token missing for refund (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    rc = payment_gateway_refund(saga->gateway, &token);\n    if (rc != 0)\n    {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Refund failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Saga Steps Array                                                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nstatic saga_step_t g_saga_steps[] = {\n    { \"COMPLIANCE_CHECK\",      step_compliance_check,  compensate_compliance   },\n    { \"RESERVE_FUNDS\",         step_reserve_funds,     compensate_reserve_funds},\n    { \"LEDGER_POST\",           step_ledger_post,       compensate_ledger_post },\n    { \"CAPTURE_FUNDS\",         step_capture_funds,     compensate_capture_funds}\n};\n\n#define SAGA_TOTAL_STEPS (sizeof(g_saga_steps) / sizeof(g_saga_steps[0]))\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Public API                                                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * disburse_stipend_run\n *\n * Execute the Disburse Stipend Saga for a given stipend request.\n *\n * return: 0 on success, or a negative errno code on failure.\n */\nint\ndisburse_stipend_run(\n    const stipend_request_t  *request,\n    compliance_service_t     *compliance,\n    payment_gateway_t        *gateway,\n    ledger_repository_t      *ledger_repo,\n    stipend_repository_t     *stipend_repo,\n    event_bus_t              *event_bus,\n    audit_logger_t           *audit,\n    retry_policy_t            retry_policy)\n{\n    if (!request || !compliance || !gateway || !ledger_repo ||\n        !stipend_repo || !event_bus || !audit)\n    {\n        return EINVAL;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /*  Instantiate saga context                                           */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    disburse_stipend_saga_t saga = {\n        .compliance   = compliance,\n        .gateway      = gateway,\n        .ledger_repo  = ledger_repo,\n        .stipend_repo = stipend_repo,\n        .event_bus    = event_bus,\n        .audit        = audit,\n        .state        = SAGA_STATE_NOT_STARTED,\n        .retry_policy = retry_policy,\n        .request      = request,\n        .steps        = g_saga_steps,\n        .step_count   = SAGA_TOTAL_STEPS,\n        .started_at   = timestamp_now()\n    };\n    uuid_generate(saga.saga_id, sizeof(saga.saga_id));\n\n    saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Saga %s (%s) started for Stipend #%s.\",\n                   saga.saga_id, SAGA_VERSION, request->stipend_id);\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /*  Forward execution                                                 */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    ssize_t current_step = 0;\n    for (; current_step < (ssize_t)saga.step_count; ++current_step)\n    {\n        const saga_step_t *step = &saga.steps[current_step];\n        size_t attempt = 0;\n\n        saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_DEBUG, \"\u2192 Executing step: %s\", step->name);\n\n        while (attempt <= saga.retry_policy.max_retries)\n        {\n            if (step->forward(&saga))\n            {\n                /* Success */\n                break;\n            }\n\n            attempt++;\n            if (attempt > saga.retry_policy.max_retries)\n            {\n                /* Abort forward flow */\n                saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_WARN,\n                               \"Step %s exhausted retry budget.\", step->name);\n                goto rollback; /* Begin compensation */\n            }\n\n            /* Wait before retry */\n            uint32_t backoff_ms = retry_policy_backoff(&saga.retry_policy, attempt);\n            saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                           \"Retrying step %s in %ums (attempt %zu)\u2026\",\n                           step->name, backoff_ms, attempt);\n\n            retry_policy_sleep(backoff_ms);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /*  Completed successfully                                            */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    saga.state = SAGA_STATE_COMPLETED;\n    saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Saga %s completed successfully.\", saga.saga_id);\n\n    stipend_event_t ev = {\n        .type            = STIPEND_EVENT_DISBURSED,\n        .stipend_request = *request\n    };\n    saga_publish_event(&saga, &ev);\n    return 0;\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Compensation / Rollback Flow                                              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nrollback:\n    saga.state = SAGA_STATE_ROLLING_BACK;\n    saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_WARN,\n                   \"Initiating rollback of Saga %s\u2026\", saga.saga_id);\n\n    for (ssize_t i = current_step; i >= 0; --i)\n    {\n        const saga_step_t *step = &saga.steps[i];\n        saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_DEBUG,\n                       \"\u21a9 Compensating step: %s\", step->name);\n\n        if (!step->compensate(&saga))\n        {\n            saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                           \"Compensation for step %s failed.\", step->name);\n            /* Compensation failures are logged, but saga continues */\n        }\n    }\n\n    saga.state = SAGA_STATE_FAILED;\n\n    stipend_event_t failed_ev = {\n        .type            = STIPEND_EVENT_DISBURSEMENT_FAILED,\n        .stipend_request = *request\n    };\n    strncpy(failed_ev.reason, \"Saga rollback completed\", sizeof(failed_ev.reason) - 1);\n    saga_publish_event(&saga, &failed_ev);\n\n    saga_log_audit(&saga, AUDIT_WARN,\n                   \"Saga %s rolled back. Stipend disbursement aborted.\",\n                   saga.saga_id);\n\n    /* Preserve original errno set by failing step */\n    return errno ? errno : ECANCELED;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  End of file                                                               */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n",

All side-effects are routed through\n *  a set of callbacks supplied by the calling application/service.  Each\n *  callback must be idempotent because the saga might retry crashed steps.\n *\n *  Every callback returns `true` on success.  On failure it returns `false`\n *  and must populate `err_out`.\n */\n\ntypedef bool (*validate_eligibility_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        saga_error_t *err_out);\n\ntypedef bool (*publish_domain_event_fn)(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n        const char                           *event_name,\n        saga_error_t                         *err_out);\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  VTable Container                                                          */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\ntypedef struct {\n    validate_eligibility_fn   validate_eligibility;\n    reserve_budget_fn         reserve_budget;\n publish_domain_event_fn   publish_domain_event;\n} stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t;\n\n/* Utility macro to check if a pointer in the vtable is missing at runtime. */\n#define _CHECK_CB(cb) do {                                                  \\\n    if ((cb) == NULL) {                                                     \\\n        if (err_out) {                                                      \\\n            err_out->code = SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL;                              \\\n            snprintf(err_out->message, sizeof(err_out->message),            \\\n                     \"Callback missing: %s\", #cb);                          \\\n        }                                                                   \\\n        return false;                                                       \\\n    } } while (0)\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Saga Public API                                                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline\nbool disburse_stipend_run(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n        saga_error_t                           *err_out);\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Implementation                                                            */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic inline\nbool disburse_stipend_run(\n        const stipend_disbursement_request_t   *req,\n        const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t *cb,\n        saga_error_t                           *err_out)\n{\n    /* Defensive programming: never trust caller. */\n    if (!req || !cb) {\n        if (err_out) {\n            err_out->code = SAGA_ERR_INTERNAL;\n            snprintf(err_out->message, sizeof(err_out->message),\n                     \"NULL argument(s) received\");\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    uint64_t reservation_id = 0;\n    uint64_t network_tx_id  = 0;\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 1. Validate eligibility                                            */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->validate_eligibility);\n    if (!cb->validate_eligibility(req, err_out)) {\n        return false; /* validation errors are final, no compensation needed */\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 2. Reserve budget (Financial-Aid allocation ledger)                */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->reserve_budget);\n    if (!cb->reserve_budget(req, &reservation_id, err_out)) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 3. Initiate transfer via payment network                           */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->initiate_transfer);\n    if (!cb->initiate_transfer(req, &network_tx_id, err_out)) {\n\n        /* ------------------------------------------------------------------\n         * Compensation Path #1: release the budget reservation\n         * ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n        saga_error_t cmp_err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err)) {\n            /* Fatal: both forward step + compensation failed */\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) {\n                *err_out = cmp_err;\n            }\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        return false; /* original error already populated by initiate_transfer */\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 4. Record ledger entry (financial book-keeping)                    */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->record_ledger_entry);\n    if (!cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT\", network_tx_id, err_out)) {\n\n        /* Compensation Path #2: reverse transfer + release budget */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->reverse_transfer);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err1 = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->reverse_transfer(network_tx_id, &cmp_err1)) {\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) *err_out = cmp_err1;\n            /* Deliberately fall through to attempt second compensation */\n        }\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err2 = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        if (!cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err2)) {\n            if (err_out && err_out->code == SAGA_OK) *err_out = cmp_err2;\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 5. Publish domain event (CQRS / Integration-Event)                 */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    _CHECK_CB(cb->publish_domain_event);\n    if (!cb->publish_domain_event(req, \"StipendDisbursed\", err_out)) {\n\n        /* Compensation Path #3: ledger reversal + reverse transfer + release budget */\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->record_ledger_entry);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->reverse_transfer);\n        _CHECK_CB(cb->release_budget);\n\n        saga_error_t cmp_err = SAGA_ERROR_INIT();\n        cb->record_ledger_entry(req, \"STIPEND_DISBURSEMENT_REVERSED\", network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n        cb->reverse_transfer(network_tx_id, &cmp_err);\n        cb->release_budget(reservation_id, &cmp_err);\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    /* 6. Success!                                                        */\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n    if (err_out) {\n        *err_out = SAGA_ERROR_INIT(); /* reset to success */\n    }\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Example: Default No-Op Callbacks for Unit-Testing                         */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n#ifdef EDUPAY_STIPEND_SAGA_ENABLE_NOOP_CALLBACKS\n\n#include <string.h>\n\n/* These compile-time helpers allow professors to run the saga in a REPL\n * without wiring external systems.  Each callback prints to stdout and\n * pretends to succeed.\n */\n\nstatic inline bool noop_validate(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] validate_eligibility\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_reserve(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                uint64_t *id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] reserve_budget\");\n    *id = 42;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_release(uint64_t id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] release_budget\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_transfer(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                 uint64_t *id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] initiate_transfer\");\n    *id = 1337;\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_reverse(uint64_t id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] reverse_transfer\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_ledger(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                               const char *type, uint64_t rel_id, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)type; (void)rel_id; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] record_ledger_entry\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool noop_publish(const stipend_disbursement_request_t *req,\n                                const char *name, saga_error_t *err) {\n    (void)req; (void)name; (void)err;\n    puts(\"[noop] publish_domain_event\");\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic const stipend_disbursement_callbacks_t STIPEND_SAGA_NOOP_CALLBACKS = {\n    .validate_eligibility = noop_validate,\n    .reserve_budget       = noop_reserve,\n    .release_budget       = noop_release,\n    .initiate_transfer    = noop_transfer,\n    .reverse_transfer     = noop_reverse,\n    .record_ledger_entry  = noop_ledger,\n    .publish_domain_event = noop_publish\n};\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_STIPEND_SAGA_ENABLE_NOOP_CALLBACKS */\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_FINANCIAL_AID_DISBURSE_STIPEND_SAGA_H */\n",

inline rmq_status_t\n_rmq_parse_reply(amqp_rpc_reply_t reply)\n{\n    switch (reply.reply_type) {\n        case AMQP_RESPONSE_NORMAL:\n            return RMQ_OK;\n\n        case AMQP_RESPONSE_LIBRARY_EXCEPTION) {\n        snprintf(pub->last_diag.broker_reply,\n                 sizeof(pub->last_diag.broker_reply),\n                 \"LIB_EXCEPTION: %s\",\n */\n\nstatic inline rmq_status_t\nrmq_publisher_init(rmq_publisher_t *pub,\n                   const char      *host,\n                   int              port,\n                   const char dashboard_projector_handle(dashboard_projector_t *proj,\n                               const domain_event_t *event) {\n    if (!proj || !event) {\n        return -1;\n    }\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&proj->mtx);\n\n    /* Ensure idempotency */\n    if (event->sequence_number <= proj->state.last_sequence_number) {\n        pthread_mutex_unlock(&proj->mtx);\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    switch (event->type) {\n    case EVENT_PAYMENT_INITIATED:\n        proj->state.total_payments++;\n        proj->state.pending_payments++;\n        break;\n\n    case EVENT_PAYMENT_SETTLED:\n        if (proj->state.pending_payments > 0) {\n            proj->state.pending_payments--;\n        }\n        if (event->data.payment_settled.success) {\n            proj->state.total_tuition +=\n                event->data.payment_settled.amount;\n        }\n        break;\n\n    case EVENT_FRAUD_ALERT:\n        proj->state.fraud_alerts++;\n        break;\n\n    default:\n        DASHBOARD_PROJECTOR_LOG(\"Unknown event type: %d\", event->type);\n        break;\n    }\n\n    proj->state.last_sequence_number = event->sequence_number;\n\n    /* Best-effort persistence; if it coordinator lives in the domain layer (Enterprise-Business Rules)\n *  and therefore must not import any framework-specific headers.\n *  It exposes a small surface-area in C so that professors can swap\n *  infrastructure (Kafka, NATS, gRPC, REST, SQL, NoSQL, etc.) without\n *  recompiling core business rules.\n *\n *  Thread-safety:\n *      All public functions are re-entrant but *not* thread-safe.\n *      Callers that share a coordinator instance *must* provide their own\n *      synchronization (e.g., inject a mutex from the application layer).\n *\n *  Memory-management:\n *      Memory is allocated only inside saga_coordinator_create().\n *      The caller is responsible for releasing resources via\n *      saga_coordinator_destroy().\n *\n *  License:\n *      MIT \u2013 Copyright \u00a9 2024 EduPay Ledger Academy\n */\n\n#ifndef EDU_PAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_CORE_SAGA_COORDINATOR_H\n#define EDU_PAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_CORE_SAGA_COORDINATOR_H\n\n/*------------------------------ System Headers -----------------------------*/\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stddef.h>\n\n/*------------------------------ Public Macros ------------------------------*/\n#define SAGA_MAX_STEPS        32     /* Upper bound to keep stack usage low */\n#define SAGA_MAX_ERROR_TEXT  128     /* Human-readable reason buffer size   */\n\n/*------------------------------- Enumerations ------------------------------*/\n/**\n * @enum saga_step_state_t\n * Represents runtime state of an individual step during a Saga execution.\n */\ntypedef enum\n{\n    SAGA_STEP_PENDING = 0,     /* Step has not been executed yet              */\n    SAGA_STEP_COMPLETED,       /* Step executed successfully                  */\n    SAGA_STEP_FAILED,          /* Step executed and returned error            */\n    SAGA_STEP_COMPENSATED,     /* Compensation executed after a failure       */\n    SAGA_STEP_COMPENSATION_FAILED /* Compensation itself failed              */\n} saga_step_state_t;\n\n/**\n * @enum saga_execution_state_t\n * High-level status of the overall Saga.\n */\ntypedef enum\n{\n    SAGA_STATE_IDLE = 0,\n    SAGA_STATE_RUNNING,\n    SAGA_STATE_ROLLING_BACK,\n    SAGA_STATE_COMPLETED,\n    SAGA_STATE_ABORTED\n} saga_execution_state_t;\n\n/*------------------------------ Forward Decls ------------------------------*/\nstruct saga_coordinator_t;\n\n/**\n * Callback invoked by a Saga step to perform its forward (happy-path) logic.\n *\n * @param step_ctx  User-supplied context pointer bound to the step.\n * @param reason    Output buffer for an error description if the step fails.\n * @param reason_len Length of the provided buffer.\n *\n * @return true  if the step succeeded and the Saga may continue.\n *         false if an error occurred; compensation will be triggered.\n */\ntypedef bool (*saga_forward_cb_t)(void *step_ctx,\n                                  char *reason,\n                                  size_t reason_len);\n\n/**\n * Callback invoked during rollback when a previous forward step failed.\n *\n * @param step_ctx  Same context pointer passed to the forward call.\n * @param reason    Output buffer for an error description if compensation\n *                  fails. When compensation fails, the Saga transitions to\n *                  SAGA_STATE_ABORTED and no further steps are attempted.\n * @param reason_len Length of the provided buffer.\n *\n * @return true  if compensation succeeded.\n *         false if compensation itself failed \u2013 requires manual intervention.\n */\ntypedef bool (*saga_compensate_cb_t)(void *step_ctx,\n                                     char *reason,\n                                     size_t reason_len);\n\n/*------------------------------ Data Structures ----------------------------*/\n/**\n * @struct saga_step_t\n * Encapsulates a single unit of work and its compensating action.\n */\ntypedef struct\n{\n    const char          *name;           /* Human-readable step identifier   */\n    saga_forward_cb_t    do_txn;         /* Forward transaction logic        */\n    saga_compensate_cb_t undo_txn;       /* Compensation logic               */\n    void                *ctx;            /* User-defined context per step    */\n    saga_step_state_t    state;          /* Runtime state                    */\n    char                 error[SAGA_MAX_ERROR_TEXT]; /* Error buffer         */\n} saga_step_t;\n\n/**\n * @struct saga_coordinator_t\n * Public handle used by application services to compose a Saga.\n */\ntypedef struct saga_coordinator_t\n{\n    saga_step_t            steps[SAGA_MAX_STEPS];\n    uint8_t                step_count;\n    uint8_t                current;      /* Index of currently executing step */\n    saga_execution_state_t state;\n} saga_coordinator_t;\n\n/*--------------------------- Public API Functions --------------------------*/\n\n/**\n * Create a fresh Saga coordinator.\n *\n * @param[out] out_handle Pointer to hold the newly-allocated coordinator.\n *\n * @return true on success; false if memory allocation fails.\n */\nbool saga_coordinator_create(saga_coordinator_t **out_handle);\n\n/**\n * Append a step to the Saga.\n *\n * @param saga     Saga instance obtained from saga_coordinator_create().\n * @param name     Null-terminated string used for logging/observability.\n * @param forward  Forward (commit) callback.\n * @param compensate Compensation (rollback) callback.\n * @param ctx      User context pointer passed untouched to both callbacks.\n *\n * @return true if the step was registered; false if capacity reached.\n */\nbool saga_coordinator_add_step(saga_coordinator_t *saga,\n                               const char        *name,\n                               saga_forward_cb_t  forward,\n                               saga_compensate_cb_t compensate,\n                               void              *ctx);\n\n/**\n * Execute the Saga end-to-end.\n *\n * The function iterates over all steps:\n *   1. Invokes each forward callback sequentially.\n *   2. On first failure, switches to rollback mode and calls compensation\n *      callbacks in reverse order for *completed* steps.\n *\n * @param saga  Saga handle.\n *\n * @return SAGA_STATE_COMPLETED on success,\n *         SAGA_STATE_ABORTED   if any compensation fails,\n *         SAGA_STATE_ROLLING_BACK if rollback succeeded but original\n *                                 forward path had a failure.\n */\nsaga_execution_state_t saga_coordinator_execute(saga_coordinator_t *saga);\n\n/**\n * Acquire details about the failure that caused a rollback or abort.\n *\n * @param saga  Saga handle.\n *\n * @return Pointer to a constant string describing the last error,\n *         or NULL if no error was recorded.\n *\n * @note The pointer becomes invalid after saga_coordinator_destroy().\n */\nconst char * saga_coordinator_last_error(const saga_coordinator_t *saga);\n\n/**\n * Release all resources held by the coordinator.\n *\n * @param saga  Pointer returned by saga_coordinator_create().\n */\nvoid saga_coordinator_destroy(saga_coordinator_t *saga);\n\n/*----------------------- Inline Convenience Functions ----------------------*/\nstatic inline bool saga_is_success(const saga_execution_state_t st)\n{\n    return st == SAGA_STATE_COMPLETED;\n}\n\nstatic inline bool saga_is_failed(const saga_execution_state_t st)\n{\n    return (st == SAGA_STATE_ROLLING_BACK) || (st == SAGA_STATE_ABORTED);\n}\n\n#endif /* EDU_PAY_LEDGER_ACADEMY_CORE_SAGA_COORDINATOR_H */\n",

       uint16_t minor;\n        uint16_t patch;\n    } version;\n    saga_step_t   steps[SAGA_MAX_STEPS];\n    uint8_t       step_count;\n} saga_definition_t;\n\n/* This is separated from _init() so that tests\n *      can mutate the command struct (e.g. tamper scenarios) and re-validate\n *      without constructing a new object.\n *\n *      Returns:\n *          true  -> looks sane\n *          false -> invalid; details in errbuf if provided\n */\nstatic inline bool\nprocess_payment_command_is_valid(const process_payment_command_t *cmd,\n                                 char *errbuf,\n                                 size_t errlen)\n{\n    if (!cmd)\n        return false;\n\n    if (cmd->student_id[0] == '\\0')\n    {\n        if (errbuf && errlen)\n            strncpy(errbuf, \"missing student_id\", errlen - 1);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (cmd->account_id[0] == '\\0')\n    {\n        if (errbuf && errlen)\n            strncpy(errbuf, \"missing account_id\", errlen - 1);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (cmd->amount.minor_units <= 0)\n    {\n        if (errbuf && errlen)\n            strncpy(errbuf, \"amount must be positive\", errlen - 1);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (!ppc_validate_iso_currency(cmd->amount.currency))\n    {\n        if (errbuf && errlen)\n            strncpy(errbuf, \"invalid currency code\", errlen - 1);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Example business rule:  cannot force settlement AND require MFA */\n    if ((cmd->flags & PPC_FLAG_FORCE_SETTLEMENT) &&\n        (cmd->flags & PPC_FLAG_MFA_REQUIRED))\n    {\n        if (errbuf && errlen)\n            strncpy(errbuf, \"mutually exclusive flags set\", errlen - 1);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n\n/*\n *  process_payment_command_clear():\n *      Zero-out all fields to protect sensitive data before freeing or\n *      re-using the struct.  Although most fields are not secret, we teach\n *      students to wipe memory that might contain personally identifiable\n *      information (PII) or payment data.\n */\nstatic inline void\nprocess_payment_command_clear(process_payment_command_t *cmd)\n{\n    if (cmd)\n        memset(cmd, 0, sizeof(*cmd));\n}\n\n#endif /* EDUPAY_BURSAR_APP_COMMANDS_PROCESS_PAYMENT_COMMAND_H */\n",

Update Projections    \u2502\n          \u2502                           \u2502                          \u2502    (Dashboard, Balances) \u2502\n          \u2502                           \u2502                          \u2502                          \u2502\n          \u2502 10. Saga COMPLETED        \u2502                          \u2502                          \u2502\n          \u2502\u25c4\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2524                          \u2502                          \u2502\n          \u2502                           \u2502                          \u2502                          \u2502\n```\n\n### 1.2 Detailed Step-by-Step Flow\n\n| Step | Actor | Action | Description |\n|------|-------|--------|-------------|\n| 1 | `financial_aid_service` | Initiates `DisburseStipendSaga` | A stipend disbursement request triggers the saga |\n| 2 | Saga Coordinator | Execute existing steps | Steps 1-4: Compliance Check, Reserve Funds, Ledger Post, Capture Funds |\n| 3 | Saga Coordinator | Query `CheckAutoPaymentEligibility` | **NEW**: Query the projections service for student consent and outstanding tuition balance |\n| 4 | `projections_service` | Return eligibility data | Returns `{auto_pay_opt_in: bool, outstanding_balance: money_t}` |\n| 5 | Saga Coordinator | Issue `ApplyStipendToTuition` command | **NEW**: If eligible, send command to `bursar_service` with stipend amount (capped at outstanding balance) |\n| 6 | `bursar_service` | Process internal payment | Credit the student's tuition account, post entries to the double-entry ledger |\n| 7 | `bursar_service` | Emit `StipendAppliedToTuition` event | **NEW**: Publish domain event to event bus |\n| 8 | Event Bus | Broadcast event | RabbitMQ/NATS distributes event to all subscribers |\n| 9 | `projections_service` | Update read models | Update dashboard balances, student account view |\n| 10 | Saga Coordinator | Mark saga COMPLETED | Entire stipend disbursement + auto-payment workflow complete |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Saga Pattern Integration\n\n### 2.1 Recommendation: Extend the Existing `DisburseStipendSaga`\n\n**Justification:**\n\nI recommend **extending** the existing `DisburseStipendSaga` rather than creating a new saga for the following reasons:\n\n1. **Transaction Unity**: The tuition auto-payment is logically part of the stipend disbursement workflow. The stipend must be successfully disbursed before it can be applied to tuition.\n\n2. **Atomicity Semantics**: If the auto-payment fails, it should not cause the stipend disbursement to fail (the stipend is already in the student's hands). However, keeping it within the same saga allows for coherent audit trails and correlation IDs.\n\n3. **Simplified Orchestration**: A single saga instance manages the entire flow, avoiding the complexity of saga-to-saga coordination or choreography.\n\n4. **Existing Infrastructure**: The current `disburse_stipend_saga.c` implementation (`src/services/financial_aid_service/application/use_cases/disburse_stipend_saga.c:367-374`) already has the step registration pattern that supports adding new steps.\n\n### 2.2 Modified Saga Steps Array\n\nThe current saga has 4 steps (lines 367-372 in `disburse_stipend_saga.c`):\n\n```c\nstatic saga_step_t g_saga_steps[] = {\n    { \"COMPLIANCE_CHECK\",      step_compliance_check,  compensate_compliance   },\n    { \"RESERVE_FUNDS\",         step_reserve_funds,     compensate_reserve_funds},\n    { \"LEDGER_POST\",           step_ledger_post,       compensate_ledger_post },\n    { \"CAPTURE_FUNDS\",         step_capture_funds,     compensate_capture_funds},\n    /* NEW: Add auto-payment step */\n    { \"APPLY_TO_TUITION\",      step_apply_to_tuition,  compensate_apply_to_tuition }\n};\n```\n\n### 2.3 New Step Implementation\n\n```c\n/* ---- Step 5: Apply Stipend to Tuition (Optional) ----------------------------- */\nstatic bool\nstep_apply_to_tuition(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO, \"Checking auto-payment eligibility...\");\n\n    /* 1. Query for eligibility (consent + balance) */\n    auto_payment_eligibility_t eligibility = {0};\n    int rc = query_auto_payment_eligibility(\n        saga->request->student.student_id,\n        &eligibility);\n\n    if (rc != 0) {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_WARN,\n                       \"Failed to check auto-payment eligibility (err=%d)\", rc);\n        /* Non-fatal: proceed without auto-payment */\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /* 2. Check consent flag */\n    if (!eligibility.auto_pay_enabled) {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                       \"Student has not opted into auto-payment. Skipping.\");\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /* 3. Check for outstanding balance */\n    if (eligibility.outstanding_tuition_balance <= 0) {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                       \"No outstanding tuition balance. Skipping auto-payment.\");\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    /* 4. Calculate amount to apply (min of stipend and balance) */\n    int64_t amount_to_apply = MIN(\n        saga->request->payout_details.amount,\n        eligibility.outstanding_tuition_balance);\n\n    /* 5. Issue command to bursar_service */\n    apply_stipend_to_tuition_cmd_t cmd = {\n        .student_id = saga->request->student.student_id,\n        .amount = {\n            .minor_units = amount_to_apply,\n            .currency = saga->request->payout_details.currency\n        },\n        .correlation_id = saga->saga_id,\n        .stipend_id = saga->request->stipend_id\n    };\n\n    rc = bursar_service_apply_stipend_to_tuition(&cmd);\n    if (rc != 0) {\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Auto-payment failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        /* Depending on business rules: fail saga or continue */\n        return true; /* Continue - stipend already disbursed */\n    }\n\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Auto-payment of %ld cents applied to tuition.\",\n                   amount_to_apply);\n\n    return true;\n}\n\nstatic bool\ncompensate_apply_to_tuition(disburse_stipend_saga_t *saga)\n{\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Reversing auto-payment (if applied)...\");\n\n    /* Issue reversal command to bursar_service */\n    int rc = bursar_service_reverse_tuition_application(\n        saga->request->student.student_id,\n        saga->saga_id);\n\n    if (rc != 0 && rc != ENOENT) { /* ENOENT = nothing to reverse */\n        saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_ERROR,\n                       \"Tuition application reversal failed (err=%d)\", rc);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. New Domain Events\n\n### 3.1 Event Definitions\n\nThe following new domain events should be defined in `src/shared_kernel/domain/events/`:\n\n#### 3.1.1 `StipendAppliedToTuition`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `financial_aid_service` (for audit)\n\n```c\n/* File: src/shared_kernel/domain/events/stipend_applied_to_tuition.h */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;                   /* Standard event header */\n    char         student_id[32];        /* Student receiving credit */\n    char         stipend_id[37];        /* Source stipend UUID */\n    char         tuition_account_id[32];/* Target tuition account */\n    money_t      amount_applied;        /* Amount credited */\n    money_t      remaining_balance;     /* Outstanding balance after */\n    char         correlation_id[37];    /* Saga correlation */\n    time_t       applied_at_utc;        /* Timestamp */\n} evt_stipend_applied_to_tuition_t;\n```\n\n#### 3.1.2 `StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed`\n\n**Publisher:** `bursar_service`\n**Consumers:** `projections_service`, `financial_aid_service` (for monitoring/alerts)\n\n```c\n/* File: src/shared_kernel/domain/events/stipend_application_failed.h */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         student_id[32];\n    char         stipend_id[37];\n    char         error_code[16];        /* Machine-readable code */\n    char         error_message[256];    /* Human-readable description */\n    char         correlation_id[37];\n    time_t       failed_at_utc;\n} evt_stipend_application_to_tuition_failed_t;\n```\n\n#### 3.1.3 `AutoPaymentConsentChanged`\n\n**Publisher:** Student profile service (or admissions)\n**Consumers:** `projections_service` (to update consent read model)\n\n```c\n/* File: src/shared_kernel/domain/events/auto_payment_consent_changed.h */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    evt_header_t hdr;\n    char         student_id[32];\n    bool         auto_pay_enabled;      /* New consent state */\n    time_t       consented_at_utc;      /* When consent was given/revoked */\n    char         consent_channel[32];   /* \"WEB_PORTAL\", \"MOBILE_APP\", etc. */\n} evt_auto_payment_consent_changed_t;\n```\n\n### 3.2 Event Catalog Update\n\nPer the existing event catalog in `docs/architecture/02_microservices_and_bounded_contexts.md:50-57`, add:\n\n```markdown\n## Event Catalog (Ubiquitous Language) - Extended\n\n* `StudentRegistered`\n* `InvoiceRaised`\n* `PaymentAuthorized`\n* `AidDisbursed`\n* `LedgerEntryPosted`\n* `SagaCompensationRequired`\n* **`StipendAppliedToTuition`**        \u2190 NEW\n* **`StipendApplicationToTuitionFailed`** \u2190 NEW\n* **`AutoPaymentConsentChanged`**      \u2190 NEW\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Persistence\n\nPer `src/services/bursar_service/infrastructure/persistence/postgres_event_store.h`, the new events will be persisted with:\n\n1. **Stream ID**: `student:{student_id}:tuition`\n2. 3,\n    EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION = 4,   /* NEW */\n    EVENT_AUTO_PAYMENT_CONSENT_CHANGED = 5  /* NEW */\n} domain_event_type_t;\n\n/* Add handler in dashboard_projector_handle() (line 292-341) */\ncase EVENT_STIPEND_APPLIED_TO_TUITION:\n    /* Update total tuition collected */\n    proj->state.total_tuition += event->data.stipend_applied.amount;\n    /* Update pending payments (decrease outstanding) */\n    if (proj->state.pending_payments > 0) {\n        proj->state.pending_payments--;\n    }\n    break;\n```\n\n#### 4.3.2 New Projection: Student Account Balance View\n\nA new projector should be created to maintain per-student balance views:\n\n**File:** `src/projections_service/event_handlers/student_balance_projector.c`\n\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    char     student_id[32];\n    int64_t  tuition_balance;      /* Outstanding amount */\n    int64_t  stipend_balance;      /* Available stipend funds */\n    bool     auto_pay_enabled;     /* Consent flag */\n    time_t   last_updated;\n} student_balance_projection_t;\n\n/* Handler for StipendAppliedToTuition */\nstatic int on_stipend_applied(const evt_stipend_applied_to_tuition_t *e) {\n    student_balance_projection_t proj;\n    load_student_projection(e->student_id, &proj);\n\n    proj.tuition_balance = e->remaining_balance.amount;\n    proj.last_updated = e->applied_at_utc;\n\n    save_student_projection(&proj);\n    return 0;\n}\n\n/* Handler for AutoPaymentConsentChanged */\nstatic int on_consent_changed(const evt_auto_payment_consent_changed_t *e) {\n    student_balance_projection_t proj;\n    load_student_projection(e->student_id, &proj);\n\n    proj.auto_pay_enabled = e->auto_pay_enabled;\n    proj.last_updated = e->consented_at_utc;\n\n    save_student_projection(&proj);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Compliance and Consent\n\n### 5.1 Regulatory Framework\n\nPer `docs/architecture/05_security_and_compliance.md` and `docs/lessons/L03_Regulatory_Compliance_in_Code.md`, the auto-payment feature must comply with:\n\n| Regulation | Requirement | Implementation |\n|------------|-------------|----------------|\n| **FERPA** | Student consent for financial data sharing | Explicit opt-in stored in student profile |\n| **PCI-DSS** | Payment data security | Tokenization of any card data involved |\n| **SOC 2** | Audit trail | Immutable event log of all consent changes and auto-payments |\n\n### 5.2 Consent Storage\n\nThe student's auto-payment consent flag should be stored as a **first-class domain entity** in the Admissions bounded context:\n\n**Location:** `src/services/admissions_service/domain/student_preferences.h`\n\n```c\ntypedef struct {\n    char     student_id[32];\n    bool     auto_pay_tuition_enabled;\n    time_t   consent_granted_at;\n    time_t   consent_revoked_at;       /* 0 if currently consented */\n    char     consent_version[16];      /* Terms version accepted */\n    char     consent_channel[32];      /* How consent was obtained */\n} student_payment_preferences_t;\n```\n\n### 5.3 Consent Check in Workflow\n\nThe consent check occurs at **Step 5** of the saga (before issuing `ApplyStipendToTuition`):\n\n```c\n/* In step_apply_to_tuition() */\n\n/* Query the student balance projection for consent flag */\nauto_payment_eligibility_t eligibility = {0};\nint rc = query_auto_payment_eligibility(\n    saga->request->student.student_id,\n    &eligibility);\n\n/* Explicit consent check - this is the compliance gate */\nif (!eligibility.auto_pay_enabled) {\n    saga_log_audit(saga, AUDIT_INFO,\n                   \"Student %s has not opted into auto-payment (consent required).\",\n                   saga->request->student.student_id);\n\n    /* Per FERPA: Do not proceed without explicit consent */\n    return true; /* Saga continues but skips auto-payment */\n}\n```\n\n### 5.4 Audit Trail Requirements\n\nEvery auto-payment action must be logged to the immutable audit trail (per `docs/architecture/05_security_and_compliance.md:22-23`):\n\n```c\n/* Required audit entries */\naudit_logger_log(audit, AUDIT_INFO, \"AUTO_PAYMENT\",\n    \"consent_verified\", student_id, saga_id,\n    \"Student consent for auto-payment verified.\");\n\naudit_logger_log(audit, AUDIT_INFO, \"AUTO_PAYMENT\",\n    \"amount_calculated\", student_id, saga_id,\n    \"Auto-payment amount: %ld cents (stipend: %ld, balance: %ld).\",\n    amount_to_apply, stipend_amount, outstanding_balance);\n\naudit_logger_log(audit, AUDIT_INFO, \"AUTO_PAYMENT\",\n    \"applied_to_tuition\", student_id, saga_id,\n    \"Stipend %s applied to tuition account %s.\",\n    stipend_id, tuition_account_id);\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Summary of Architectural Decisions\n\n| Decision | Rationale |\n|----------|-----------|\n| **Extend existing saga** vs. new saga | Maintains transaction unity; stipend disbursement and auto-payment are logically coupled |\n| **Query projections for eligibility** | CQRS pattern: read models are optimized for queries; avoid hitting the write model |\n| **Consent as first-class entity** | FERPA compliance requires auditable consent records; not a simple boolean flag |\n| **Step 5 is non-blocking** | Auto-payment failure should not fail the stipend disbursement (student still gets money) |\n| **Compensating action reverses ledger entry** | Saga pattern requires idempotent compensation; ledger reversal creates compensating entries |\n| **New projector for student balances** | Separation of concerns; dashboard KPIs vs. individual student account views |\n\n---\n\n## 8.
